## <a name="app-startup-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-862">Erros de inicialização do aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-862">App startup errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-863">No Visual Studio, um projeto ASP.NET Core usa como padrão a hospedagem [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) durante a depuração.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-863">In Visual Studio, an ASP.NET Core project defaults to [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) hosting during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-864">Uma *falha de processo 502,5* que ocorre ao depurar localmente pode ser diagnosticada usando o Conselho neste tópico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-864">A *502.5 Process Failure* that occurs when debugging locally can be diagnosed using the advice in this topic.</span></span>

### <a name="40314-forbidden"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-865">403,14 proibido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-865">403.14 Forbidden</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-866">Falha ao iniciar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-866">The app fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-867">O seguinte erro é registrado em log:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-867">The following error is logged:</span></span>

```
The Web server is configured to not list the contents of this directory.
```

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-868">O erro geralmente é causado por uma implantação quebrada no sistema de hospedagem, que inclui qualquer um dos seguintes cenários:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-868">The error is usually caused by a broken deployment on the hosting system, which includes any of the following scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-869">O aplicativo é implantado na pasta incorreta no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-869">The app is deployed to the wrong folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-870">O processo de implantação não moveu todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo para a pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-870">The deployment process failed to move all of the app's files and folders to the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-871">O arquivo de *web.config* está ausente na implantação ou o conteúdo do arquivo de *web.config* está malformado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-871">The *web.config* file is missing from the deployment, or the *web.config* file contents are malformed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-872">Execute as seguintes etapas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-872">Perform the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-873">Exclua todos os arquivos e pastas da pasta de implantação no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-873">Delete all of the files and folders from the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-874">Reimplante o conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do aplicativo no sistema de hospedagem usando o método normal de implantação, como o Visual Studio, o PowerShell ou a implantação manual:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-874">Redeploy the contents of the app's *publish* folder to the hosting system using your normal method of deployment, such as Visual Studio, PowerShell, or manual deployment:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-875">Confirme se o arquivo de *web.config* está presente na implantação e se seu conteúdo está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-875">Confirm that the *web.config* file is present in the deployment and that its contents are correct.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-876">Ao hospedar no serviço Azure App, confirme se o aplicativo está implantado na `D:\home\site\wwwroot` pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-876">When hosting on Azure App Service, confirm that the app is deployed to the `D:\home\site\wwwroot` folder.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-877">Quando o aplicativo é hospedado pelo IIS, confirme se o aplicativo está implantado no **caminho físico** do IIS mostrado nas **configurações básicas** do **Gerenciador do IIS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-877">When the app is hosted by IIS, confirm that the app is deployed to the IIS **Physical path** shown in **IIS Manager**'s **Basic Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-878">Confirme se todos os arquivos e pastas do aplicativo estão implantados comparando a implantação no sistema de hospedagem ao conteúdo da pasta de *publicação* do projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-878">Confirm that all of the app's files and folders are deployed by comparing the deployment on the hosting system to the contents of the project's *publish* folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-879">Para obter mais informações sobre o layout de um aplicativo ASP.NET Core publicado, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-879">For more information on the layout of a published ASP.NET Core app, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-880">Para obter mais informações sobre o arquivo de *web.config* , consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-880">For more information on the *web.config* file, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span></span>

### <a name="500-internal-server-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-881">Erro interno de servidor 500</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-881">500 Internal Server Error</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-882">O aplicativo é iniciado, mas um erro impede o servidor de atender à solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-882">The app starts, but an error prevents the server from fulfilling the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-883">Esse erro ocorre no código do aplicativo durante a inicialização ou durante a criação de uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-883">This error occurs within the app's code during startup or while creating a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-884">A resposta poderá não conter nenhum conteúdo, ou a resposta poderá ser exibida como um *500 – Erro Interno do Servidor* no navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-884">The response may contain no content, or the response may appear as a *500 Internal Server Error* in the browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-885">O Log de Eventos do Aplicativo geralmente indica que o aplicativo iniciou normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-885">The Application Event Log usually states that the app started normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-886">Da perspectiva do servidor, isso está correto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-886">From the server's perspective, that's correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-887">O aplicativo foi iniciado, mas não é capaz de gerar uma resposta válida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-887">The app did start, but it can't generate a valid response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-888">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no servidor ou habilite o log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core para solucionar o problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-888">Run the app at a command prompt on the server or enable the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log to troubleshoot the problem.</span></span>

### <a name="5025-process-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-889">Falha de processo 502.5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-889">502.5 Process Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-890">O processo de trabalho falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-890">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-891">O aplicativo não foi iniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-891">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-892">O [Módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta iniciar o processo de trabalho, mas falhar ao iniciar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-892">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the worker process but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-893">A causa de uma falha de inicialização do processo geralmente pode ser determinada com base em entradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo e no log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-893">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-894">Uma condição de falha comum é o aplicativo configurado incorretamente, direcionado a uma versão da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core que não está presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-894">A common failure condition is the app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-895">Verifique quais versões da estrutura compartilhada do ASP.NET Core estão instaladas no computador de destino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-895">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-896">A *estrutura compartilhada* é o conjunto de assemblies (arquivos *. dll*) instalado no computador e referenciado por um metapacote como `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-896">The *shared framework* is the set of assemblies (*.dll* files) that are installed on the machine and referenced by a metapackage such as `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-897">A referência do metapacote pode especificar a versão mínima necessária.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-897">The metapackage reference can specify a minimum required version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-898">Saiba mais em [A estrutura compartilhada](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-898">For more information, see [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-899">A página do erro *502.5 – Falha no Processo* é retornada quando um erro de configuração de hospedagem ou do aplicativo faz com que o processo de trabalho falhe:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-899">The *502.5 Process Failure* error page is returned when a hosting or app misconfiguration causes the worker process to fail:</span></span>

### <a name="failed-to-start-application-errorcode-0x800700c1"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-900">Falha ao iniciar o aplicativo (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-900">Failed to start application (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span></span>

```
EventID: 1010
Source: IIS AspNetCore Module V2
Failed to start application '/LM/W3SVC/6/ROOT/', ErrorCode '0x800700c1'.
```

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-901">O aplicativo falhou ao ser iniciado porque o assembly do aplicativo (*.dll*) não pôde ser carregado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-901">The app failed to start because the app's assembly (*.dll*) couldn't be loaded.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-902">Esse erro ocorre quando há uma incompatibilidade de número de bits entre o aplicativo publicado e o processo w3wp/iisexpress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-902">This error occurs when there's a bitness mismatch between the published app and the w3wp/iisexpress process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-903">Confirme se a configuração de 32 bits do pool de aplicativos está correta:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-903">Confirm that the app pool's 32-bit setting is correct:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-904">Selecione o pool de aplicativos no **Pools de Aplicativos** do Gerenciador do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-904">Select the app pool in IIS Manager's **Application Pools**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-905">Selecione **Configurações Avançadas** em **Editar Pool de Aplicativos** no painel **Ações**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-905">Select **Advanced Settings** under **Edit Application Pool** in the **Actions** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-906">Defina **Habilitar Aplicativos de 32 bits**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-906">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications**:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-907">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86), defina o valor como `True`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-907">If deploying a 32-bit (x86) app, set the value to `True`.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-908">Se estiver implantando um aplicativo de 64 bits (x64), defina o valor como `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-908">If deploying a 64-bit (x64) app, set the value to `False`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-909">Confirme se não há um conflito entre uma `<Platform>` Propriedade do MSBuild no arquivo de projeto e o bit de bits publicado do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-909">Confirm that there isn't a conflict between a `<Platform>` MSBuild property in the project file and the published bitness of the app.</span></span>

### <a name="connection-reset"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-910">Redefinição de conexão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-910">Connection reset</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-911">Se um erro ocorrer após os cabeçalhos serem enviados, será tarde demais para o servidor enviar um **500 – Erro Interno do Servidor** no caso de um erro ocorrer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-911">If an error occurs after the headers are sent, it's too late for the server to send a **500 Internal Server Error** when an error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-912">Isso geralmente acontece quando ocorre um erro durante a serialização de objetos complexos para uma resposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-912">This often happens when an error occurs during the serialization of complex objects for a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-913">Esse tipo de erro é exibida como um erro de *redefinição de conexão* no cliente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-913">This type of error appears as a *connection reset* error on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-914">O [Log de aplicativo](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) pode ajudar a solucionar esses tipos de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-914">[Application logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) can help troubleshoot these types of errors.</span></span>

### <a name="default-startup-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-915">Limites de inicialização padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-915">Default startup limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-916">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) é configurado com um *startupTimeLimit* padrão de 120 segundos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-916">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) is configured with a default *startupTimeLimit* of 120 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-917">Quando deixado no valor padrão, um aplicativo pode levar até dois minutos para iniciar antes que uma falha do processo seja registrada em log pelo módulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-917">When left at the default value, an app may take up to two minutes to start before the module logs a process failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-918">Para obter informações sobre como configurar o módulo, veja [Atributos do elemento aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-918">For information on configuring the module, see [Attributes of the aspNetCore element](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-919">Solucionar problemas no serviço Azure App</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-919">Troubleshoot on Azure App Service</span></span>

[!INCLUDE [Azure App Service Preview Notice](~/includes/azure-apps-preview-notice.md)]

### <a name="application-event-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-920">Log de eventos do aplicativo (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-920">Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-921">Para acessar o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo, use a folha **Diagnosticar e solucionar problemas** no portal do Azure:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-921">To access the Application Event Log, use the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-922">No portal do Azure, abra o aplicativo nos **Serviços de Aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-922">In the Azure portal, open the app in **App Services**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-923">Selecione **Diagnosticar e solucionar problemas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-923">Select **Diagnose and solve problems**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-924">Selecione o título **Ferramentas de Diagnóstico**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-924">Select the **Diagnostic Tools** heading.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-925">Em **Ferramentas de Suporte**, selecione o botão **Eventos do Aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-925">Under **Support Tools**, select the **Application Events** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-926">Examine o erro mais recente fornecido pela entrada *IIS AspNetCoreModule* ou *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* na coluna **Origem**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-926">Examine the latest error provided by the *IIS AspNetCoreModule* or *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* entry in the **Source** column.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-927">Uma alternativa ao uso da folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** é examinar o arquivo de Log de Eventos do Aplicativo diretamente usando o [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-927">An alternative to using the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade is to examine the Application Event Log file directly using [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-928">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-928">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-929">Selecione o **botão &rarr; ir** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-929">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-930">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-930">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-931">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-931">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-932">Abra a pasta **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-932">Open the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-933">Selecione o ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *eventlog.xml*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-933">Select the pencil icon next to the *eventlog.xml* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-934">Examine o log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-934">Examine the log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-935">Role até o final do log para ver os eventos mais recentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-935">Scroll to the bottom of the log to see the most recent events.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-in-the-kudu-console"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-936">Execute o aplicativo no console do Kudu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-936">Run the app in the Kudu console</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-937">Muitos erros de inicialização não produzem informações úteis no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-937">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-938">Você pode executar o aplicativo no Console de Execução Remota do [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) para descobrir o erro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-938">You can run the app in the [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) Remote Execution Console to discover the error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-939">Abra **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **Ferramentas de Desenvolvimento**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-939">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-940">Selecione o **botão &rarr; ir** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-940">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-941">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-941">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-942">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-942">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-32-bit-x86-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-943">Testar um aplicativo de 32 bits (x86)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-943">Test a 32-bit (x86) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-944">**Versão atual**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-944">**Current release**</span></span>

1. `cd d:\home\site\wwwroot`
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-945">Executar o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-945">Run the app:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-946">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-946">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

     ```dotnetcli
     dotnet .\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-947">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-947">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

     ```console
     {ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-948">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando todos os erros, é canalizada para o console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-948">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-949">**Implantação dependente da estrutura em execução em uma versão de visualização**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-949">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-950">*Requer a instalação da extensão de site de runtime do ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-950">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-951">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` é a versão de runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-951">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-952">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-952">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-953">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando todos os erros, é canalizada para o console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-953">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-64-bit-x64-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-954">Testar um aplicativo de 64 bits (x64)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-954">Test a 64-bit (x64) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-955">**Versão atual**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-955">**Current release**</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-956">Se o aplicativo for uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd) de 64 bits (x64):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-956">If the app is a 64-bit (x64) [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>
  1. `cd D:\Program Files\dotnet`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-957">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-957">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-958">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-958">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>
  1. `cd D:\home\site\wwwroot`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-959">Execute o aplicativo: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-959">Run the app: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-960">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando todos os erros, é canalizada para o console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-960">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-961">**Implantação dependente da estrutura em execução em uma versão de visualização**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-961">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-962">*Requer a instalação da extensão de site de runtime do ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-962">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-963">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` é a versão de runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-963">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-964">Execute o aplicativo: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-964">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-965">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando todos os erros, é canalizada para o console do Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-965">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-966">Log de stdout do módulo ASP.NET Core (serviço Azure App)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-966">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-967">O log de stdout do Módulo do ASP.NET Core geralmente registra mensagens de erro úteis não encontradas no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-967">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-968">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-968">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-969">Navegue até a folha **Diagnosticar e resolver problemas** no portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-969">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-970">Em **SELECIONAR CATEGORIA DE PROBLEMA**, selecione o botão **Aplicativo Web Inoperante**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-970">Under **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY**, select the **Web App Down** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-971">Em **Soluções Sugeridas** > **Habilitar o Redirecionamento de Log de Stdout**, selecione o botão para **Abrir o Console do Kudu para editar o Web.Config**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-971">Under **Suggested Solutions** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection**, select the button to **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-972">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, abra as pastas no caminho **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-972">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-973">Role para baixo para revelar o arquivo *web.config* na parte inferior da lista.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-973">Scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-974">Clique no ícone de lápis ao lado do arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-974">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-975">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-975">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-976">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-976">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-977">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-977">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-978">Retorne ao portal do Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-978">Return to the Azure portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-979">Selecione a folha **Ferramentas Avançadas** na área **FERRAMENTAS DE DESENVOLVIMENTO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-979">Select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-980">Selecione o **botão &rarr; ir** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-980">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-981">O console do Kudu é aberto em uma nova janela ou guia do navegador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-981">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-982">Usando a barra de navegação na parte superior da página, abra **Console de depuração** e selecione **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-982">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-983">Abra a pasta **LogFiles**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-983">Select the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-984">Inspecione a coluna **Modificado em** e selecione o ícone de lápis para editar o log de stdout com a data da última modificação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-984">Inspect the **Modified** column and select the pencil icon to edit the stdout log with the latest modification date.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-985">Quando o arquivo de log é aberto, o erro é exibido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-985">When the log file opens, the error is displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-986">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-986">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-987">No **Console de Diagnóstico** do Kudu, retorne para o caminho **site** > **wwwroot** para revelar o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-987">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, return to the path **site** > **wwwroot** to reveal the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-988">Abra o arquivo **web.config** novamente, selecionando o ícone de lápis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-988">Open the **web.config** file again by selecting the pencil icon.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-989">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-989">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-990">Selecione **Salvar** para salvar o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-990">Select **Save** to save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-991">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-991">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-992">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-992">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-993">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-993">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-994">Somente use o log de stdout para solucionar problemas de inicialização de aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-994">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-995">Para registro em log geral em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core após a inicialização, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-995">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-996">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-996">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="monitoring-blades"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1001">Folhas de monitoramento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1001">Monitoring blades</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1029">Dentro dos dados de fluxo de log, a causa do erro é indicada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1029">Within the log stream data, the cause of the error is indicated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1034">Confira a [seção de Rastreamentos de solicitação com falha no tópico Habilitar o log de diagnósticos para aplicativos Web no Serviço de Aplicativo do Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) e as [Perguntas frequentes do desempenho do aplicativo para Aplicativos Web no Azure: como ativar o rastreamento de solicitação com falha?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) para obter mais informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1034">See [Failed request traces section of the Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service topic](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) and the [Application performance FAQs for Web Apps in Azure: How do I turn on failed request tracing?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) for more information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1035">Para obter mais informações, veja [Habilitar log de diagnósticos para aplicativos Web no Serviço de Aplicativo do Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1035">For more information, see [Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1036">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1036">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1037">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1037">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1038">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1038">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1039">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1039">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1040">Solução de problemas no IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1040">Troubleshoot on IIS</span></span>

### <a name="application-event-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1041">Log de eventos do aplicativo (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1041">Application Event Log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1042">Acesse o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1042">Access the Application Event Log:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1043">Abra o menu Iniciar, procure *Visualizador de eventos* e selecione o aplicativo **Visualizador de eventos** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1043">Open the Start menu, search for *Event Viewer*, and select the **Event Viewer** app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1044">No **Visualizador de Eventos**, abra o nó **Logs do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1044">In **Event Viewer**, open the **Windows Logs** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1045">Selecione **Aplicativo** para abrir o Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1045">Select **Application** to open the Application Event Log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1046">Procure erros associados ao aplicativo com falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1046">Search for errors associated with the failing app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1047">Os erros têm um valor *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS* ou *Módulo AspNetCore do IIS Express* na coluna *Origem*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1047">Errors have a value of *IIS AspNetCore Module* or *IIS Express AspNetCore Module* in the *Source* column.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-at-a-command-prompt"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1048">Execute o aplicativo em um prompt de comando</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1048">Run the app at a command prompt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1049">Muitos erros de inicialização não produzem informações úteis no Log de Eventos do Aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1049">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1050">Você pode encontrar a causa de alguns erros ao executar o aplicativo em um prompt de comando no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1050">You can find the cause of some errors by running the app at a command prompt on the hosting system.</span></span>

#### <a name="framework-dependent-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1051">Implantação dependente de estrutura</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1051">Framework-dependent deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1052">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação dependente de estrutura](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1052">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1053">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o aplicativo, executando o assembly do aplicativo com *dotnet.exe*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1053">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app by executing the app's assembly with *dotnet.exe*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1054">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name> : `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1054">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1055">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1055">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1056">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1056">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1057">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1057">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1058">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1058">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

#### <a name="self-contained-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1059">Implantação autocontida</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1059">Self-contained deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1060">Se o aplicativo é uma [implantação autossuficiente](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1060">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1061">Em um prompt de comando, navegue até a pasta de implantação e execute o arquivo executável do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1061">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app's executable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1062">No comando a seguir, substitua o nome do assembly do aplicativo por \<assembly_name> : `<assembly_name>.exe` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1062">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `<assembly_name>.exe`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1063">A saída do console do aplicativo, mostrando eventuais erros, é gravada na janela do console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1063">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1064">Se os erros ocorrerem ao fazer uma solicitação para o aplicativo, faça uma solicitação para o host e a porta em que o Kestrel escuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1064">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1065">Usando o host e a porta padrão, faça uma solicitação para `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1065">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1066">Se o aplicativo responde normalmente no endereço do ponto de extremidade do Kestrel, a probabilidade de o problema estar relacionado à configuração de hospedagem é maior e, de estar relacionado ao aplicativo, menor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1066">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1067">Log de stdout do módulo ASP.NET Core (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1067">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1068">Para habilitar e exibir logs de stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1068">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1069">Navegue até a pasta de implantação do site no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1069">Navigate to the site's deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1070">Se a pasta *logs* não estiver presente, crie-a.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1070">If the *logs* folder isn't present, create the folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1071">Para obter instruções sobre como habilitar o MSBuild para criar a pasta *logs* na implantação automaticamente, veja o tópico [Estrutura de diretórios](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1071">For instructions on how to enable MSBuild to create the *logs* folder in the deployment automatically, see the [Directory structure](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure) topic.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1072">Edite o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1072">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1073">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `true` e altere o caminho **stdoutLogFile** para apontar para a pasta *logs* (por exemplo, `.\logs\stdout`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1073">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to point to the *logs* folder (for example, `.\logs\stdout`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1074">`stdout` no caminho é o prefixo do nome do arquivo de log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1074">`stdout` in the path is the log file name prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1075">Uma extensão de arquivo, uma ID do processo e um carimbo de data/hora são adicionados automaticamente quando o log é criado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1075">A timestamp, process id, and file extension are added automatically when the log is created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1076">Usando `stdout` como o prefixo do nome do arquivo, um arquivo de log típico é nomeado *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1076">Using `stdout` as the file name prefix, a typical log file is named *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1077">Verifique se a identidade do pool de aplicativos tem permissões de gravação para a pasta *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1077">Ensure your application pool's identity has write permissions to the *logs* folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1078">Salve o arquivo *web.config* atualizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1078">Save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1079">Faça uma solicitação ao aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1079">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1080">Navegue até a pasta *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1080">Navigate to the *logs* folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1081">Localize e abra o log de stdout mais recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1081">Find and open the most recent stdout log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1082">Estude o log em busca de erros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1082">Study the log for errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1083">Desabilite o registro em log de stdout quando a solução de problemas for concluída:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1083">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1084">Edite o arquivo *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1084">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1085">Defina **stdoutLogEnabled** para `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1085">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1086">Salve o arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1086">Save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1087">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1087">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1088">Falha ao desabilitar o log de stdout pode levar a falhas de aplicativo ou de servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1088">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1089">Não há limites para o tamanho do arquivo de log ou para o número de arquivos de log criados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1089">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1090">Para registro em log de rotina em um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, use uma biblioteca de registro em log que limita o tamanho do arquivo de log e realiza a rotação de logs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1090">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1091">Para obter mais informações, veja [provedores de log de terceiros](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1091">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-developer-exception-page"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1092">Habilitar a página de exceção do desenvolvedor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1092">Enable the Developer Exception Page</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1093">A  [variável de ambiente `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` pode ser adicionada ao web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) para executar o aplicativo no ambiente de desenvolvimento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1093">The `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` [environment variable can be added to web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) to run the app in the Development environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1094">Desde que o ambiente não seja substituído na inicialização do aplicativo por `UseEnvironment` no compilador do host, definir a variável de ambiente permite que a [Página de Exceções do Desenvolvedor](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) apareça quando o aplicativo é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1094">As long as the environment isn't overridden in app startup by `UseEnvironment` on the host builder, setting the environment variable allows the [Developer Exception Page](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) to appear when the app is run.</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore processPath="dotnet"
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll"
      stdoutLogEnabled="false"
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout">
  <environmentVariables>
    <environmentVariable name="ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT" value="Development" />
  </environmentVariables>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1095">Configurar a variável de ambiente para `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` só é recomendado para servidores de preparo e de teste que não estejam expostos à Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1095">Setting the environment variable for `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` is only recommended for use on staging and testing servers that aren't exposed to the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1096">Remova a variável de ambiente do arquivo *web.config* após a solução de problemas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1096">Remove the environment variable from the *web.config* file after troubleshooting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1097">Para obter informações sobre como definir variáveis de ambiente no *web.config*, confira [Elemento filho environmentVariables de aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1097">For information on setting environment variables in *web.config*, see [environmentVariables child element of aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span></span>

### <a name="obtain-data-from-an-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1098">Obter dados de um aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1098">Obtain data from an app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1099">Se um aplicativo for capaz de responder às solicitações, obtenha as solicitações, conexão e dados adicionais do aplicativo que usar o middleware embutido de terminal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1099">If an app is capable of responding to requests, obtain request, connection, and additional data from the app using terminal inline middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1100">Para saber mais e obter um código de exemplo, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1100">For more information and sample code, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1101">Aplicativo lento ou suspenso (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1101">Slow or hanging app (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1102">Um *despejo* é um instantâneo da memória do sistema e pode ajudar a determinar a causa de uma falha de aplicativo, de inicialização ou de um aplicativo lento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1102">A *crash dump* is a snapshot of the system's memory and can help determine the cause of an app crash, startup failure, or slow app.</span></span>

#### <a name="app-crashes-or-encounters-an-exception"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1103">O aplicativo falha ou encontra uma exceção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1103">App crashes or encounters an exception</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1104">Obter e analisar um despejo de memória do [WER (Relatório de Erros do Windows)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1104">Obtain and analyze a dump from [Windows Error Reporting (WER)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1105">Crie uma pasta para armazenar os arquivos de despejo de memória em `c:\dumps`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1105">Create a folder to hold crash dump files at `c:\dumps`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1106">O pool de aplicativos deve ter acesso para gravação à pasta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1106">The app pool must have write access to the folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1107">Execute o [script EnableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1107">Run the [EnableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1108">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1108">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps w3wp.exe c:\dumps
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1109">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1109">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps dotnet.exe c:\dumps
     ```

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1110">Execute o aplicativo sob as condições que causam a falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1110">Run the app under the conditions that cause the crash to occur.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1111">Após a falha, execute o [script DisableDumps do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1111">After the crash has occurred, run the [DisableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1112">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1112">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps w3wp.exe
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1113">Se o aplicativo usa o [modelo de hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), execute o script para *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1113">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps dotnet.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1114">Depois que um aplicativo falhar e a coleta de despejo de memória for concluída, o aplicativo terá permissão para encerrar normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1114">After an app crashes and dump collection is complete, the app is allowed to terminate normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1115">O script do PowerShell configura o WER para coletar até cinco despejos de memória por aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1115">The PowerShell script configures WER to collect up to five dumps per app.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1116">Os despejos de memória podem usar uma grande quantidade de espaço em disco (até vários gigabytes cada).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1116">Crash dumps might take up a large amount of disk space (up to several gigabytes each).</span></span>

#### <a name="app-hangs-fails-during-startup-or-runs-normally"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1117">O aplicativo trava, falha durante a inicialização ou executa normalmente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1117">App hangs, fails during startup, or runs normally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1118">Quando um aplicativo *paralisa* (para de responder, mas não falha), falha durante a inicialização ou é executado normalmente, consulte [arquivos de despejo no modo de usuário: escolhendo a melhor ferramenta](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) para selecionar uma ferramenta apropriada para produzir o despejo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1118">When an app *hangs* (stops responding but doesn't crash), fails during startup, or runs normally, see [User-Mode Dump Files: Choosing the Best Tool](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) to select an appropriate tool to produce the dump.</span></span>

#### <a name="analyze-the-dump"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1119">Analisar o despejo de memória</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1119">Analyze the dump</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1120">Um despejo de memória pode ser analisado usando várias abordagens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1120">A dump can be analyzed using several approaches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1121">Para obter mais informações, confira [Analisando um arquivo de despejo de memória do modo de usuário](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1121">For more information, see [Analyzing a User-Mode Dump File](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span></span>

## <a name="clear-package-caches"></a><span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1122">Limpar caches de pacote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1122">Clear package caches</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1123">Um aplicativo em funcionamento pode falhar imediatamente após a atualização do SDK do .NET Core no computador de desenvolvimento ou a alteração das versões do pacote no aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1123">A functioning app may fail immediately after upgrading either the .NET Core SDK on the development machine or changing package versions within the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1124">Em alguns casos, pacotes incoerentes podem interromper um aplicativo ao executar atualizações principais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1124">In some cases, incoherent packages may break an app when performing major upgrades.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1125">A maioria desses problemas pode ser corrigida seguindo estas instruções:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1125">Most of these issues can be fixed by following these instructions:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1126">Exclua as pastas *bin* e *obj*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1126">Delete the *bin* and *obj* folders.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1127">Limpe os caches de pacote executando [dotnet NuGet local All--Clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) de um shell de comando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1127">Clear the package caches by executing [dotnet nuget locals all --clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) from a command shell.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1128">Limpar caches de pacote também pode ser feito com a ferramenta de [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) e executar o comando `nuget locals all -clear` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1128">Clearing package caches can also be accomplished with the [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) tool and executing the command `nuget locals all -clear`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1129">*nuget.exe* não é uma instalação fornecida com o sistema operacional Windows Desktop e devem ser obtidos separadamente do [site do NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1129">*nuget.exe* isn't a bundled install with the Windows desktop operating system and must be obtained separately from the [NuGet website](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1130">Restaure e recompile o projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1130">Restore and rebuild the project.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="7fcf1-1131">Exclua todos os arquivos na pasta de implantação no servidor antes de reimplantar o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7fcf1-1131">Delete all of the files in the deployment folder on the server prior to redeploying the app.</span></span>
